                <div n="21" type="adhyāya">
                    <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 21, collation]</head>



                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.1">
                        <label>1.21.1</label>
                         || athāto vraṇapraśnaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.3">
                        <label>1.21.3</label>
                         vātapittaśleṣmāṇa eva dehe sambhavahetavo bhavanti || tair evāsyāvyāpanair
                        adhomadhyorddhasanniviṣṭaiḥ śarīram idan dhāryate| agāram iva sthūṇābhir
                        ataś ca tristhūṇam ity āhur ity eke| ta eva ca vyāpannāḥ pralayahetavo
                        bhavanti tad ebhiḥ śoṇitacaturtthaiḥ sambhavasthitipralayeṣv apy avirahitaṃ
                        śarīram bhavati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.4">
                        <label>1.21.4</label>
                         bhavati cātra ||
                        <caesura/>
                         nartte dehaḥ kaphād asti na ca pittān na mārutāt |
                        <caesura/>
                         śoṇitād api vā nityan deham etais tu dhāryate ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.5">
                        <label>1.21.5</label>
                         tatra vā gatigandhopādāno dhātuḥ | tapa santāpe | śliṣa āliṅgane | eṣāṃ
                        kṛdvihitaiḥ pratyayair vvātaṃ pittaṃ śleṣmā iti rūpāṇi bhavanti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.6">
                        <label>1.21.6</label>
                         teṣāṃ sthānāny ata ūrddhvam vakṣyāmaḥ || tatra samāsena vāyuḥ
                        śroṇīgudasaṃśrayaḥ | pakvāmāsayamadhyastham pittasya | āmāsayaḥ śleṣmaṇaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.7">
                        <label>1.21.7</label>
                         ataḥ param pañcadhā vibhajyante | tatra vātasya vātavyādhike vakṣyāmaḥ |
                        pittasya yakṛtplīhānau hṛdayan dṛṣṭis tvag iti | pūrvvoktan tu śleṣmaṇas
                        tūrasaḥ kaṇṭhaḥ śiraḥ sandhaya iti || etāni khalu doṣasthānāny avyāpannānām
                        bhavanti | pūrvvoktañ ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.8">
                        <label>1.21.8</label>
                         visargādānavikṣepaiḥ somasūryānilā yathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         dhārayanti jagaddehaṅ kaphapittānilās tathā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.9">
                        <label>1.21.9</label>
                         tatra jijñāsyate || kim pittavyatirekeṇānyo 'gnirutāho pittam evāgnir iti |
                        atrocyate | na khalu pittavyatirekeṇānyo 'gnir upalabhyate | āgneyatvāt
                        pitte dahanapacanādiṣu pravarttamāno 'gnivad upacāraḥ kriyante ntaragnir iti
                        | kṣiṇe vāgniguṇe tatsamānadravyopayogād ativṛddhe śītakriyopayogād āgamāc
                        ca paśyāmo na khalu pittavyatirekeṇānyo 'gnir iti | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.10">
                        <label>1.21.10</label>
                         tat tu dṛṣṭahetukena viśeṣeṇa pakvāmāsayamadhyasthaṃ caturvvidham apy annam
                        pacati vivecayati ca doṣarasamūtrapurīṣāṇi | tatrastham eva cātmaśaktyā
                        śeṣāṇām pittasthānānāṃ śarīrasya cāgnikarmmaṇānugrahaṅ karoti | tasmin pitte
                        pācako 'gnir iti saṃjñā || yakṛtplīhnoḥ pittan tasmin rañjako gnir iti
                        saṃjñā sa rasasya rāgakṛd uktaḥ | yat tu hṛdistham pittan tasmin sādhako
                        'gnir iti saṃjñā śobhitaprārthitamanorathasādhanakṛd uktaḥ || yat tu dṛṣṭyām
                        pittaṃ tasminn ālocako 'gnir iti saṃjñā sa rūpagrahaṇe dhikṛtaḥ || yat tu
                        tvaci pittan tasya bhrājako 'gnir iti saṃjñā so
                        'bhyaṅgaparisekāvagāhālayanādīnāṃ kriyādravyādīnāṃ pācayitā |||| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.11">
                        <label>1.21.11</label>
                         bhavati cātra ||
                        <caesura/>
                         pittaṃ tīkṣṇan dravam pūtinīlam pītan tathaiva ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         uṣṇaṅ kaṭurasañ caiva vidagdhan tv amlam iṣyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.12">
                        <label>1.21.12</label>
                         ata ūrdhvaṃ śleṣmasthānāny anuvyākhyāsyāmaḥ || tatrāmāsayaḥ
                        pittāsayasyopari tatpratyanīkatvād ūrdhvagatitvāt tejasaś candra ivādityasya
                        sa caturvvidhasyāhārasyādhāraḥ sa ca tatraudakair guṇaiḥ praklinno
                        bhinnasaṃghātas sukhajaro bhavati || </l>



                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.13">
                        <label>1.21.13</label>
                         mādhuryāt picchilatvāc ca prakleditvāt tathaiva ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         āmāsaye sambhavati śleṣmā madhuraśītalaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.14">
                        <label>1.21.14</label>
                         sa tatra sthitaḥ svaśaktyā śeṣāṇāṃ śleṣmasthānānāṃ
                        śarīrasyodakakarmmaṇānugrahaṅ karoti || uraḥsthas tu trikasandhāraṇam
                        ātmavīryyeṇānnarasasahitena hṛdayāvalambanam varaṇañ ca karoti | kaṇṭhasthas
                        tu jihvendriyasya saumyatvāt samyagrasajñāne vivarttate || śiraḥsthas tu
                        snehasantarppaṇādhikṛtatvād indriyāṇām ātmavīryyeṇānugrahaṃ karoti ||
                        sandhisthas tu sandhisaṃśleṣāt sarvvaṃ sandhisaṃśleṣāt sarvvasandhyagranuhaṅ
                        karoti || </l>



                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.15">
                        <label>1.21.15</label>
                         bhavati cātra ||
                        <caesura/>
                         śleṣmā śveto guru snigdhaḥ picchilaḥ śīta eva ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         madhuraś cāvidagdhaḥ syād vidagdho lavaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.16">
                        <label>1.21.16</label>
                         śoṇitasthānaprāgabhihitaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.17">
                        <label>1.21.17</label>
                         anuṣṇaśītam madhuraṃ snigdhaṃ raktañ ca varṇataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śoṇitaṅ guru visraṃ syād vidāhaś cāsya pittavat || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.18">
                        <label>1.21.18</label>
                         etāni khalu doṣasthānāny atra sañcīyante doṣāḥ | prāk sañcayahetur uktaḥ ||
                        sañcitānāṃ khalu doṣāṇāṃ stabdhapūrṇṇakoṣṭhatā pītāvabhāsatā mandoṣmatā
                        cāṅgānāṃ gauravam ālasyañ ceti liṅgāni bhavanti | tatra prathamaḥ kriyākālaḥ
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.19">
                        <label>1.21.19</label>
                         ata ūrdhvam prakopakāraṇāni vakṣyāmaḥ | tatra
                        balavadvigrahātivyavāyavyāyāmapratapanapradhāvanābhighātalaṅghanaplavanaprataraṇajāgaraṇahayagajarathaprayāṇātikaṭukakaṣāyatiktalaghurūkṣaśītavīryyaśuṣkaśākavallūrakoradūṣaśyāmākanīvāramudgamasūrāḍhakīhareṇuniṣpāvānaśanavātamūtrapurīṣaśukravathūdgāraccharddibāṣpavegavighātādibhir
                        vviśeṣair vvāyuḥ prakopam āpadyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.20">
                        <label>1.21.20</label>
                         sa śītābhraprayāteṣu gharmmārtte ca viśeṣataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         pratyūṣasy aparāhṇe ca jīrṇṇānte ca prakupyati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.21">
                        <label>1.21.21</label>
                         krodhaśokabhayāyāsopavāsavidagdhamaithunopagamanakaṭvamlalavaṇoṣṇatīkṣṇarūkṣalaghuvidāhitilatailapiṇyākakulatthasarṣapātasīharitaśākavarāhamatsyājāvikamāṃsadadhimastutakrasauvīrakasurāmlaphalakaṭvaraprabhṛtibhi<subst>
                            <del rend="erased">ḥ</del>
                        </subst>r vviśeṣaiḥ pittam prakopam āpadyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.22">
                        <label>1.21.22</label>
                         taduṣṇe voṣṇakāle ca ghanānte ca viṣeśataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         madhyāhne cārddharātre ca jīryyaty anne ca kupyati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.23">
                        <label>1.21.23</label>
                         divāsvapno vyāyāmālasyamadhurāmlalavaṇasnigdhaśīta<add place="margin
                            bottom"
                        >guru</add>picchilābhiṣyandihāyanakayavanaiṣadhotkaṭamāṣagodhūmatilapiṣṭavikṛtadugdhadadhikṛśarapāyasekṣuvikārānūpodakamāṃsavasābisamṛṇālakaserukaśṛṅgāṭakamadhuravallīphalasamasanādhyaśanaprabhṛtibhir
                        vviśeṣaiḥ śleṣmā prakopam āpadyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.24">
                        <label>1.21.24</label>
                         sa śīte śītakāle ca vasante ca viśeṣataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         pūrvvāhṇe ca pradoṣe ca bhuktamātre prakupyati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.25">
                        <label>1.21.25</label>
                         pittaprakopaṇair eva cābhīkṣṇaṃ dravasnigdhagurubhiś cāhārair
                        ddivāsvapnakrodhānalātapaśramābhighātājīrṇṇaviruddhādhyaśanaprabhṛtibhir
                        vviśeṣair raktam prakopam āpadyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.26">
                        <label>1.21.26</label>
                         yasmād raktam vinā doṣair nna kadācit prakupyati |
                        <caesura/>
                         tasmāt tasya yathādoṣaṅ kālam vidyāt prakopanaiḥ || </l>



                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.27">
                        <label>1.21.27</label>
                         teṣān tu prakopāt koṣṭhatodasañcaraṇāmlīkādāhapipāsānnadveṣahṛdayotkledā
                        bhavanti | tatra dvitīyaḥ kriyākālaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.28">
                        <label>1.21.28</label>
                         ata ūrdhvam prasaraṃ vakṣyāmaḥ | teṣām ebhir ātaṅkaviśeṣaiḥ prakupitānām
                        piṣṭakiṇvodakasamavāya ivābhyudgatānām prasaro bhavati | teṣām vāyur
                        ggatimattvāt prasaraṇahetuḥ | saty apy ācaitanye sa hi rajobhūyiṣṭhaḥ |
                        rajaś ca pravarttakam bhāvānām yathā mahānudakasañcayo 'tipravṛddhatvāt |
                        setum avadāryāparair udakair vvyāmiśraḥ sarvvataḥ pradhāvaty evan doṣāḥ |
                        ekaikaśo dvandvaśaḥ samastāḥ śoṇitasahitā vā tatra vātaḥ pittaṃ śleṣmā
                        śoṇitaṃ | vātapitte | vātaśleṣmāṇau | pittaśleṣmāṇau | vātaśoṇite |
                        pittaśoṇite | śleṣmaśoṇite | vātapittaśoṇitāni | vātaśleṣmaśoṇitāni |
                        pittaśleṣmaśoṇitāni | vātapittakaphāḥ | vātapittakaphaśoṇitānīti | evam
                        pañcadaśadhā prasaranti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.29">
                        <label>1.21.29</label>
                         kṛtsne 'rdhe 'vayave cāpi dehasya kupito bhṛśam |
                        <caesura/>
                         doṣo vikāram bhajate megho vṛṣṭim ivāmbare || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.30">
                        <label>1.21.30</label>
                         nātyarthaṅ kupitaś cāpi līno mārggeṣu ti<g ref="#newa-gap-filler"/>ṣṭhati |
                        <caesura/>
                         niḥpratyanīkaḥ kālena hetum āsādya kupyati || </l>




                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.31">
                        <label>1.21.31</label>
                         nagatasya vātavat kriyāvibhāgaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.32">
                        <label>1.21.32</label>
                         evaṃ prakṣubhitānāṃ prasaratāṃ vimārgagamanam āṭopo dhūmāyanam arocakaś
                        charddir iti liṅgāni bhavanti | tatra tṛtīyaḥ kriyākālaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.33">
                        <label>1.21.33</label>
                         ata ūrddhvaṃ sthānasaṃśrayam vakṣyāmaḥ | evaṃ khalu prasṛtās tāṃs tāñ
                        charīrapradeśān āgamya tāṃs tān vyādhīñ janayanti | taṃ prati pratirogaṃ
                        vakṣyāmaḥ | te yadodar dhayaḥ sanniveśaṅ kurvanti te
                        gulmavṛdhyudarāgnisaṅgānāhavisūcikātīsāraprabhṛtīñ janayanti || bastigatāḥ
                        pramehāśmarīmūtrāghātamūtradoṣaprabhṛtīn || gudagatās tu
                        bhagandarārsaprabhṛtīn || meḍhragatās tu
                        parivarttikāpadaṃśaśūkadoṣaprabhṛtīn || vṛṣaṇagatā vṛṣaṇavṛddhīn ||
                        ūrddhvajatrugatā ūrddhvagā galagaṇḍāpacīprabhṛtīn || tvaṅmānsasoṇitagatāḥ
                        kṣudrarogān kuṣṭhādīṃ visarpāṃś ca || māṃsagatā
                        granthyapacyarbudagalagaṇḍālajīprabhṛtīn || asthigatā
                        vidradhyanuśayīprabhṛtīn || pādagatāḥ ślīpadavātasoṇitaprabhṛtīn ||
                        sarvagatāḥ jvaraśukradoṣasarvāṅgarogaprabhṛtīn || evam anyeṣv api sthāneṣu
                        rogāṇāṃ doṣasanniveśaṃ jānīyāt || teṣām evam abhisanniviṣṭānām
                        pūrvarūpaprādurbhāvo bhavati | tatra caturthaḥ kriyākālaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.34">
                        <label>1.21.34</label>
                         ata ūrddhvaṃ vyādhidarsanam vakṣyāmaḥ ||
                        sophārbudagranthividradhivisarpādīnāṃ pravyaktalakṣaṇatā
                        jvarātīsāraprabhṛtīnāñ ca | tatra pañcamakriyākālaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.35">
                        <label>1.21.35</label>
                         ata ūrddhvam asyāvadīrṇṇasya vraṇabhāvam āpannasya ṣaṣṭhaḥ kriyākālaḥ ||
                        jvarātīsāraprabhṛtīnāñ ca dīrghakālānubandhaḥ | tatrāpratikriyamāṇo
                        sādhyatām upaiti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.36">
                        <label>1.21.36</label>
                         bhavati cātra ||
                        <caesura/>
                         sañcayañ ca prakopañ ca prasaraṃ sthānasaṃśrayaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         vyaktim bhedañ ca yo vetti doṣāṇāṃ sa bhaved bhiṣak || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.37">
                        <label>1.21.37</label>
                         sañcaye pahṛtā doṣā labhante nottarā gatīḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         te tūttarāsu gatiṣu bhavanti balavattarāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.38">
                        <label>1.21.38</label>
                         sarvair bhāvais tṛbhir vāpi dvābhyām ekena vā punaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         saṃsarge kupitaḥ kruddhaṃ doṣaṃ doṣo nudhāvati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.39">
                        <label>1.21.39</label>
                         saṃsarge yo garīyāṃ syād upakramyaḥ sa vai bhavet |
                        <caesura/>
                         śeṣadoṣāvirodhena sannipāte tathaiva ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.40">
                        <label>1.21.40</label>
                         vraṇe tu yasmād rūḍhe pi vraṇavastu na naśyati |
                        <caesura/>
                         ādehadhāraṇāj jantor vraṇas tasmān nirucyata iti</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.trailer">|| 21 || ||</l>

                </div>

                <div n="22" type="adhyāya">
                    <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 22, collation]</head>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.22.1">
                        <label>1.22.1</label>
                         athāto vraṇāsrāvavijñānīyam vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.22.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.22.3">
                        <label>1.22.3</label>
                         tvaṅmānsasirāsnāyvasthisandhikoṣṭhamarmāṇy aṣṭau vraṇavastūni bhavanti |
                        atra sarvavraṇasanniveśaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.22.4">
                        <label>1.22.4</label>
                         tatrādyaikavastusanniveśī tvagbhedī vraṇaḥ sūpacaro bhavati | śeṣās tv
                        āsrāvā vijñeyāḥ | ya evam uttiṣṭhanty avadīvyante ca | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.22.5">
                        <label>1.22.5</label>
                         āyataś caturasro vṛttas tripuṭaka iti vraṇākṛtisamāsaḥ | viśeṣatas tu
                        vikṛtākṛ𑑛tayo durupakramā bhavanti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.22.6">
                        <label>1.22.6</label>
                         sarva eva vraṇāḥ kṣipraṃ saṃrohanty ātmavatāṃ subhiṣagbhiś copakrāntāḥ |
                        anātmavatāṃ majñaiś copakrāntāḥ praduṣyanti pravṛdvatvād doṣāṇāṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.22.7">
                        <label>1.22.7</label>
                         tatrātisamvṛto vivṛtaḥ kaṭhinotimātram atimṛdur utsannovasannaḥ śītotyuṣṇaḥ
                        kṛṣṇaraktapītaśuklādivarṇṇaiṣv apy arthavarṇṇaḥ
                        pūtimāṃsasirāsnāyupratipūrṇṇaḥ pūtipūyāśrāvī ūnmārgy utsaṅgy
                        amanojñadarśanagandhotyarthavedanāvān
                        dāhapākarāgakaṇḍūśophapiṭakopadrutotyarthaduṣṭaśoṇitasrāvī
                        dīrghakālānubandhī ceti duṣṭavraṇaliṅgāni || tatra doṣocchrāyam avekṣya
                        yathāsvaṃ prakurvīta || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.22.8a">
                        <label>1.22.8</label>
                         atha sarvāsrāvām vakṣyāmaḥ | tatra ghṛṣṭāsu chinnāsu vā tvakṣu tvaksphuṭite
                        bhinnevadārite vā salilaprakāśo bhavaty āsrāvaḥ kiñcid visraḥ pītāvabhāsaś
                        ca | māṃsagate tu sarpiḥ prakāśaḥ sāndraḥ svetaḥ picchilaś ca | sirāgatas tu
                        sadyaś chinnāsu sirāsu raktātipravṛttiḥ pakvāsu ca toyanāḍībhir ivāgamanaṃ
                        pūyasya āśrāvaś cātra tanur vicchinnaḥ sapheno vasāpratimaḥ saraktaś ca |
                        snāyugatas tu snigdho ghanaḥ siṃghaṇakapratimaḥ saraktaś ca | asthigatas tu
                        asthiny abhihate sphuṭite bhinne 'vadārite vā doṣabhakṣitatvāc chuktidhautam
                        ivābhāti asthiniḥsāraś ca bhavati | āsrāvaś cātra tanur vicchinno
                        majjāmiśraḥ sarudhirasnigdhaś ca sandhigatas tu pīḍyamāno na pravarttate |
                        tathākuñcanaprasāraṇonnāmanavināmanoskāsanapradhāvanaiḥ sravati | āsrāvaś
                        cātra tanur vicchinnaḥ picchilovalambī sarudhironmathitaś ca bhavati |
                        koṣṭhagatas tu mūtrapurīṣapūyarudhirodakāni sravati | marmagatas tu nocyate
                        tvagādiṣv evāvaruddhatvāt || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.22.8b"/>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.22.9"/>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.22.10"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.22.11">
                        <label>1.22.11</label>
                         atha sarvavraṇavedanām vakṣyāmaḥ ||
                        todanabhedanacchedanatāḍanāvamanthanāyāmanavikṣepaṇacumucumāyananirddarśanāvabhañjanasphoṭanavidāraṇotpāṭanakampanavividhaśūlaviśleṣaṇavikiraṇapūraṇastambhanaśvapanākuñcanāṅkuśikāḥ
                        sambhavanti | vividhā vā yatra muhurmuhur vedanā āgacchanti tam vātikam iti
                        vidyāt | ūṣācoṣaparidāhadhūmāyanāni yatrāṅgārāvakīrṇṇam iva vedanā sarujaṃ
                        tīkṣṇasampātipacyate yatra coṣmābhir vṛddhir bhavati kṣate kṣārāvasiktavac
                        ca yatra vedanāviśeṣāḥ ghotāta m paittikam iti viṃdyāt | pittavad
                        raktasamutthañ jānīyāt | viśeṣo raktado raktasrāvaś ca bhavati |
                        kaṇḍūrgurutvaṃ suptatā svedolpavedanatvaṃ stambhaḥ śaityañ ca yatra taṃ
                        ślaiṣmikam iti vidyāt | yatra sarvavedanāsamutpattis taṃ sānnipātikam iti
                        vidyāt || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.22.12">
                        <label>1.22.12</label>
                         ata ūrddhvaṃ sarvavarṇṇām vakṣyāmaḥ | bhasmakaposthivarṇṇaḥ
                        paruṣoruṇavarṇṇaḥ kṛṣṇa iti mārutajasya | nīlaḥ śyāvo haritaḥ pītaḥ kṛṣṇo
                        raktaḥ piṅgala iti pittaraktasamutthayoḥ | śvetasnigdhaḥ pāṇḍur iti
                        śleṣmajasya | sarvavarṇṇopetaḥ sānnipātika || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.22.13">
                        <label>1.22.13</label>
                         bhavati cātra ślokaḥ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         na kevalaṃ vraṇeṣūkto vedanāvarṇṇasaṅgrahaḥ
                        <caesura/>
                         sarvaśophavikāreṣu vraṇaval lakṣayed bhiṣag iti</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.22.trailer"> || 22 || ❈ ||</l>
                </div>

                <div n="23" type="adhyāya">
                    <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 23, collation]</head>



                    <l xml:id="SS.1.23.1">
                        <label>1.23.1</label>
                         athātaḥ kṛtyākṛtyavidhiṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.23.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.23.3">
                        <label>1.23.3</label>
                         tatra vayasthānāṃ dṛḍhānāṃ prāṇavatāṃ satvavatām ātmavatāñ ca sucikitsyā
                        vraṇā bhavanti || ekaikasmin vā puruṣe yatraitad guṇapañcakaṃ bhavati tasya
                        khalu sādhanīyatamāḥ tatra vayasthānāṃ pratyagradhātutvād āśu vraṇasaṃroho
                        bhavati | dṛḍhānāṃ sthirabahumāṃsatvāc chastram avacāryamāṇaṃ sirāsnāyvādīn
                        viśeṣān na prāpnoti prāṇavatām vedanābhighātāhārayantraṇādibhir nna glānir
                        bbhavati | satvavatān dāruṇair api kriyāviśeṣair nna vyathā bhavati |
                        ātmavatām punar mmitāhāravihārādibhir upadeśair nnānyathā matiḥ pravarttate
                        | sarvvañ caiṣāṃ sādhur bbhavati | tasmād eṣāṃ sukhasādhanīyatamāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.23.4">
                        <label>1.23.4</label>
                         ta eva viparītaguṇāḥ | vṛddhakṛṣālpaprāṇabhīruṣv anātmavatsu ca draṣṭavyāḥ
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.23.5">
                        <label>1.23.5</label>
                         sphikpāyuprajananalalāṭagaṇḍauṣṭhaphalakoṣodarajatrumukhābhyantarasaṃsthāḥ
                        sukharopaṇīyā vraṇāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.23.6">
                        <label>1.23.6</label>
                         akṣidantanāsāapāṅgaśrotranābhijaṭharasevanīnitambapārśvakukṣistanakakṣasandhibhāgagatāḥ
                        saphenapūyānilaraktavāhinontaḥśalyāś ca duścikitsyāḥ ||
                        romāntopanakhamanmajaṅghāsthisaṃśritāś ca bhagandaram api cāntarmmukhaṃ
                        sevanīkakcupasthasaṃśritam iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.23.7">
                        <label>1.23.7</label>
                         kuṣṭhinām viṣajuṣṭānāṃ śoṣiṇām madhumehinām |
                        <caesura/>
                         vraṇāḥ kṛcchreṇa sidhyanti yeṣāñ cāpi vraṇe vraṇāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.23.8">
                        <label>1.23.8</label>
                         avapāṭikāniruddhaprakāsasanniruddhagudajaṭharagranthikṣatakrimayaḥ
                        pratiśyāyajāḥ koṣṭhajāś ca tvagdoṣiṇām pramehiṇām vā ye pratikṣateṣu
                        dṛśyante śarkkarā sikatāmehī vātakuṇḍālikāṣṭhīlā
                        dantaśarkkaropakuśakaṇṭhakāśālūkaniṣkoṣaṇadūṣitā dantaveṣṭā
                        visarppāsthikṣatoraḥkṣatayaś ca yāpyāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.23.9">
                        <label>1.23.9</label>
                         || bhavanti cātra ||
                        <caesura/>
                         sādhyā yāpyatvam āyānti yāpyāś cāsādhyatām iyuḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         asādhyāś cādaduḥ prāṇān narāṇām akriyāvatāṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.23.10">
                        <label>1.23.10</label>
                         evaṃ yāpyam vijānīyāt kriyā dhārayate hitaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kriyāyān tu nivṛttāyāṃ sadya eva vinaśyati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.23.11">
                        <label>1.23.11</label>
                         prāptā kriyā dhārayate yāpyavyādhitam āturaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         prapatantam ivāgāram viṣkambhaḥ sādhuyojitaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.23.11.1">
                        <label>1.23.11.1</label>
                         kriyāyān tu nivṛttāyāṃ sadya eva vinaśyati |<anchor n="SS.1.23.11.1-n1"/>
                        <caesura/>
                         viṣkambhapatanād yadvad gṛhasya patanaṃ dhruvaṃ ||</l>

                    <ab corresp="#SS.1.23.11.1" type="apparatus">
                        <list type="notes">
                            <item corresp="#SS.1.23.11.1-n1">This repeats 1.23.10cd.</item>
                        </list>
                    </ab>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.23.12">
                        <label>1.23.12</label>
                         ata ūrddhvam asādhyān padekṣyāmaḥ || māṃsapiṇḍavad udgatāḥ
                        prasekinontaḥpūyā vedanāvantaḥ | aśvāpānavad udvṛttauṣṭhāḥ kecit kaṭhinā
                        gośṛṅgavad udgatāḥ | mṛdumāṃsaprarohāḥ | apare duṣṭarudhirāśrāviṇaḥ |
                        tantupicchilāsrāviṇo vā madhyonnatāḥ | kecid avasannaśuṣiraparyantāḥ |
                        śaṇatūlavat snāyujālavanto durddarśanāḥ | vasāmedomajjāmastuluṅgāśrāviṇaś ca
                        | doṣasamutthā pītāsitamūtrapurīṣavātavāhinaś ca koṣṭhaprāptāḥ | ta
                        evobhayato bhāgaṃ vraṇamukheṣu pūyaraktanirvvāhiṇaḥ kṣīṇamāṃsānāñ ca
                        sarvvato gatayas tv aṇumukhān māṃsabudbudavantaḥ saśabdavātavāhinaś ca
                        śiraḥkaṇṭhasthāḥ | kṣīṇamāṃsānāñ ca pūyarudhiranirvvāpinaḥ |
                        arocakāvipākakāsaśvāsopadravayuktāḥ | bhinne ca śiraḥkapāla yatra
                        mastuluṅgadarśanan tridoṣaliṅgaprādurbhāvaḥ | kāsaśvāsau vā yasyeti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.23.13">
                        <label>1.23.13</label>
                         bhavanti cātra ślokāḥ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         vasāmedo 'tha majjānam mastuluṅgañ ca yaḥ sravet |
                        <caesura/>
                         āgantujo vraṇaḥ sidhyen na sidhyed doṣasambhavaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.23.14">
                        <label>1.23.14</label>
                         amarmmopahite deśe sirāsaṃdhyasthivarjjite |
                        <caesura/>
                         vikāro yo 'nuparyeti tad asādhyasya lakṣaṇaṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.23.15">
                        <label>1.23.15</label>
                         krameṇopacayaṃ prāpto dhātūn anugataḥ śanaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         na śakyam unmūlayituṃ vṛddho vṛkṣa ivāmayaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.23.16">
                        <label>1.23.16</label>
                         sa sthiratvān mahattvāc ca dhātvanukramaṇena ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         nihantyauṣadhavīryāṇi balavattvāt tathaiva ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.23.17">
                        <label>1.23.17</label>
                         ato yo viparītaḥ syāt sukhasādhyaḥ sa ucyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         abaddhamūlaḥ kṣupako yadvad utpāṭane sukhaṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.23.18">
                        <label>1.23.18</label>
                         tribhir ddoṣair anākrāntaḥ śyāvauṣṭhaḥ piḍakī samaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         avedano nirāsrāvo vraṇaḥ śuddha iti smṛtaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.23.19">
                        <label>1.23.19</label>
                         kapotavarṇṇapratimo yasyānte kledavarjjitāḥ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         sthirāś ca piṭakāvanto rohatīti tam ādiśet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.23.20">
                        <label>1.23.20</label>
                         rūḍhavarmmāṇam agranthim aśūnam arujam vraṇaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tvaksavarṇṇaṃ samatalaṃ samyag rūḍham vinirddiśet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.23.21">
                        <label>1.23.21</label>
                         doṣaprakopād vyāyāmād abhighātād ajīrṇṇataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         harṣāt krodhād bhayād vāpi vraṇo rūḍho 'pi dīryate || 23 || </l>


                </div>


                <div n="24" type="adhyāya">

                    <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 24]</head>

                    <note xml:lang="en">[collation based on N (1.24.1–7) and K (1.24.7–12).]</note>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.24.1">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.24.1</label>
                         athāto vyādhisamuddeśīyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.24.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.24.3">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.24.3</label>
                         dvividhā vyādhayaḥ śastrasādhyāḥ snehādikriyāsādhyāś ca | tatra
                        śastrasādhyeṣu snehādikriyā na pratiṣidhyate snehādikriyāsādhyeṣu
                        śastrakarma na kriyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.24.4">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.24.4</label>
                         asmiṃs tu śāstre sarvatra sāmānyāt sarveṣāṃ vyādhīnāṃ
                        yathāsthaulyenāvarodhaḥ kriyate | prāgabhihitaṃ tadduḥkhasaṃyogād vyādhir
                        iti || tac ca duḥkhaṃ trividhaṃ | ādhyātmikam ādhibhautikam ādhidaivikam iti
                        | tac ca duḥkhaṃ saptavidhe vyādhāv upanipatati | saptavidhās tu vyādhayaḥ |
                        tad yathā ādibalapravṛttāḥ | janmabalapravṛttāḥ | doṣabalapravṛttāḥ |
                        saṃghātabalapravṛttāḥ | daivabalapravṛttāḥ | svabhāvabalapravṛttāḥ | iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.24.5">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.24.5</label>
                         tatrādibalapravṛttā nāma śukraśoṇitadoṣānvayāḥ | kuṣṭhārśaḥprabhṛtayaḥ | te
                        'pi dvivividhā mātṛjāpitṛjāś ca || janmabalapravṛttā nāma ye mātur apacārāt
                        paṅgujaḍajātyandhamūkabadhiraminminavāmanaprabhṛtayo jāyante te dvividhā
                        rasakṛtā dauhṛdāpacārakṛtāś ca || doṣabalapravṛttā nāma ya ātaṅkāpacārakṛtās
                        te dvividhāḥ | śārīrā mānasāś ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.24.7a">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.24.7a</label>
                         kālabalapravṛttā nāma ye śītoṣṇavātavarṣāprabhṛtibhiḥ samutpannās te 'pi
                        dvividhā vyāpannā avyāpannāś ca ||<anchor n="SS.1.24.7a-n1"/></l>

                    <ab corresp="#SS.1.24.7a" type="apparatus">
                        <list type="notes">
                            <item corresp="#SS.1.24.7a-n1">In the 1931 vulgate edition, this passage
                                comes after 1.24.6, before <foreign>daivabalapravṛttā
                                …</foreign>.</item>
                        </list>
                    </ab>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.24.6">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.24.6</label>
                         saṃghātabalapravṛttā nāma ya āgantava ādhibhautikās te dvividhāḥ |
                        durbalasya balavadvigrahāc chastrādikṛtāś ca |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.24.7">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.24.7</label>
                         daivabalapravṛttā nāma ya aupasargikā dvividhā abhicārābhiśāpābhiṣaṅgajāḥ
                        || svabhāvabalapravṛttā nāma kṣutpipāsājarāmṛtyunidrāprabhṛtaya iti | te 'pi
                        dvividhā rakṣakṛtā arakṣakṛtāḥ | rakṣakṛtaḥ kālakṛtaḥ | arakṣakṛto
                        'kālakṛtaḥ || atra sarvatra vyādhyuparodhaḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.24.8">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.24.8</label>
                         sarveṣāṃ ca vyādhīnām vātapittaśleṣmāṇa eva mūlaṃ | talliṅgatvād
                        dṛṣṭaphalatvād āgamāc ca paśyāmaḥ | yathā hi kṛtsnaṃ vikārajātaṃ
                        vaiśvarūpyeṇa vyavasthitaṃ | satva<pc> </pc>rajas<pc> </pc>tamāṃsy
                        avyatiricya varttante | evam eva kṛtsnaṃ vikārajātaṃ vaiśvarūpyeṇāvasthitaṃ
                        | avyatiricya vātapittaśleṣmāṇo varttante | doṣadhātumalasaṃsargād
                        āyatanaviśeṣān nimittataś caiṣāṃ vikalpo bhavati | doṣadūṣiteṣv atyarthañ ca
                        dhātuṣu saṃjñā bhavati || rasajo 'yaṃ raktajo 'yaṃ māṃsajo 'yaṃ medojo 'yaṃ
                        asthijo 'yaṃ majjajo 'yaṃ śukrajo 'yaṃ vyādhir iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.24.9">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.24.9</label>
                         aśraddhārocakapipāsāṅgamardajvarahṛllāsātṛptigauravapāṇḍurogasrotorodhakārśyavairasyāṅgasādāḥ
                        | akālapalitatimiradarśanarasadoṣajā vikārāḥ || kuṣṭhavisarpapiṭakās
                        tilakālakanacchavyaṅgamasakanīlikākoṭhaplīhagulmavidradhyarśo
                        'rbudāsṛgdararaktapittaprabhṛtayo raktadoṣāt || gudamukhameḍhrapākāś
                        cādhimāṃśārbbudārsopajihvopakuśagalaśuṇḍikāmāṃśasaṃghātoṣṭhaprakopagalagaṇḍagaṇḍamālāprabhṛtayo
                        māṃsadoṣāt ||
                        granthivṛddhigalagaṇḍārbbudoṣṭhaprakopamadhumehātisthaulyaprabhṛtayo
                        medodoṣāt || adhyasthidantāsthitodaśūlādayo 'sthidoṣāt ||
                        tamodarśamūrcchābhramapārśvagauravahṛcchūlasthūlamūlorujambheti majjadoṣāt
                        || klaibyam apraharṣaś ca śukradoṣāt || tvagdoṣaḥ saṅgo 'tipravṛrttir vā
                        malānāṃ malāyatanadoṣāt || indriyāṇāṃ ayathā pravṛttir apravṛttir vā
                        indriyāyatanadoṣād ity eṣa samāso vistaraṃ nimittāni caiṣām pratirogam
                        vakṣyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.24.10">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.24.10</label>
                         bhavati cātra ||
                        <caesura/>
                         kupitānāṃ hi doṣāṇāṃ śarīre paridhāvatāṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yatra saṅgaḥ savaiguṇyād<anchor n="SS.1.24.10-n1"/> vyādhis tatropajāyate
                        || </l>

                    <ab corresp="#SS.1.24.10" type="apparatus">
                        <list type="notes">
                            <item corresp="#SS.1.24.10-n1">Ḍalhaṇa pointed out that others read
                                    <foreign>svavaiguṇyād</foreign> (instead of
                                    <foreign>khavaiguṇyād</foreign>).</item>
                        </list>
                    </ab>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.24.11">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.24.11</label>
                         bhūyo 'tra jijñāsate | kim vātapittaśleṣmāṇāṃ jvarātisārādīnāṃ ca nityaṃ
                        saṃsleṣaḥ paricchedo veti | yadi nityaṃ saṃśleṣaḥ syān nityāturā eva
                        sarvaprāṇinaḥ syuḥ | athāpi anyathābhāvo vātādīnāṃ jvarādīnāṃ cānyatra
                        varttamānasyānyasya liṅgaṃ na bhavatīti | kṛtvā vātādayo jvarādīṇāṃ mūlānīti
                        tan na || atrocyate || doṣān pratyākhyāya jvarādayo na bhavanti | atha ca
                        nityaṃ sambandhaḥ | yathā hi vidyudvātāsanivarṣaṇyākāśaṃ pratyākhyāya na
                        bhavanti | satyapyākāse kadācic ca na bhavanti | atha ca nimittato bhavanti
                        | taraṅgabudbudādayaś codakaviśeṣāḥ | evam vātādīnāṃ jvarādīnāñ ca na
                        nityasaṃśleṣo na vicchedaḥ śāśvatikaḥ | atha ca nimittataḥ | tebhya
                        evotpattir iti || </l>



                    <l xml:id="SS.1.24.12">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.24.12</label>
                         vikāram parimāṇañ ca saṃkhyā caiṣāṃ pṛthak pṛthak |
                        <caesura/>
                         vistareṇottare tantre sarvā bādhāṃ pracakṣmaha iti || || </l>


                </div>

                        <anchor n="SS.1.25.3-4-n1"/>chedyās tu
                        bhagandarārśorbudaduṣṭavraṇanāḍīcarmakīlatilakālakamedogranthiśleṣmanimittāś
                        cāmas tathā māṃsasirāsnāyukothamāṃsakandīmāṃsāsthigatam api ca śalyam
                        uttavaḥ śataponako jatumaṇir valmīkamadhūṣodhimāṃsaḥ
                        māṃsasaṃghātagalaśuṇḍikā ity evam ādayo vikārāḥ || </l>

                        <label>1.25.5-8</label>
                         bhedyās tu sarvajamṛte vidradhyanuśayī pramehapiṭakā granthayaś ca visarpāś
                        cāditas trayas trayo vṛddhayaś ca vidārikāvamanthau puṣkarikānāḍyastanarogāś
                        ca sahopadaṃśaiḥ śophāś cāsarvasarāḥ prāyaśaḥ kṣudrarogās tathā
                        tālupuppuṭatuṇḍikerīgilāyuprabhṛtayo ntaḥ pūyaśalyāḥ pañca medaḥ samutthā
                        aśmarīhetor bastiś ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.25.17-28">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.25.17-28</label>
                         kaphagranthir alpapāliḥ karṇṇasadyovraṇaś ca yaḥ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         śirolalāṭākṣikṛṭakarṇṇeṣv anāsāgaṇḍakṛkāṭikā |
                        <caesura/>
                         bāhūdarasphikṣāyuprajananamuṣkādiṣu pradeseṣv acaleṣu māṃsavatsu ca śīvyet
                        | janukurparajaṃghādiṣu pracaleṣv alpamāṃseṣu na sīvyet | vāyunirvāhino
                        ntalohitaśalyāḥ saviṣāṃś ca tatra vās īvyaṃ vraṇam abhisamīkṣya
                        celāsthipāṃsutṛṇaromaśuṣkaraktādīny apohotkṛtyākṛṣya yathāsthānaṃ
                        sthāyayitvā snāyusūtravālānāṃ manyatamena sīvyet | saṇāśmantakamūrvātaśīnāṃ
                        vā valkalaiḥ | sūcyas tu tisra upadiśyante | dvyaṅgulā tryaṅgulā
                        dhanuvakreti | tatra māṃsaleṣv avakāśeṣu tryasrāḥ satvāsthisv alpamāṃseṣu ca
                        dvyaṅgulā vṛttā yat kāmāsamayor marmasu ca dhanuvat cakrārdhaṃ tṛtīyāṃguleti
                        || phuṇi kātūnasevanyāveṃllitakaṃ rajagranthibandhaṃ ceti | samāsena
                        sevanavikalpāḥ | teṣān nāmabhir evākṛtayaḥ prāyeṇa vyākhyātāḥ teṣāṃ prahāram
                        āsādyopayogāṃ budhyāvekṣya na cātisannikṛṣṭāṃ viprakṛṣṭām alpagrāhiṇīm
                        atibahu grāhiṇīm vā sūcīm pātayet ||

                        bhavati cātra ||

                <div n="26" type="adhyāya">
                    <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 26, collation]</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.26.1">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.26.1</label>
                         athātaḥ pranaṣṭaśalyavijñānīyam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>



                    <l xml:id="SS.1.26.3">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.26.3</label>
                         atha śalyahiṃsāyān dhātus tasya yat pratyayasya śalyam iti rūpam bhavati | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.26.4">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.26.4</label>
                         tad dvividhaṃ śārīram āgantukaṃ ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.26.5">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.26.5</label>
                         sarvaśarīrābādhakaraṃ śalyaṃ tadihopadiśyata ity ataḥ śalyaśāstram || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.26.6">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.26.6</label>
                         tatra śārīrāṇi dantanakharomādīni | dhātavo na malā doṣāś ca duṣṭāḥ
                        āgantūni śarīraśalyavyatirekeṇa yāvanto bhāvāḥ duḥkham utpādayanti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.26.6.1"> bhavati cātra ||
                        <caesura/>
                         śarīre sarvaśalyānāṃ gatayaḥ pañcadhā smṛtāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         ṛjvāgatam avāñcīnaṃ tiryag ūrdhvam adhogataṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.26.7"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.26.8"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.26.9-10">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.26.9</label>
                         tāni vegakṣayāt pratighātād vā tvagādiṣu vraṇavastuṣv avatiṣṭhante
                        dhamanīsroto 'sthivivarapeśīprabhṛtiṣu vā śarīrapradeśeṣu ||
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.26.10</label>
                         tatra śalyalakṣaṇam ucyamānam upadhāraya | tat tu dvividhaṃ sāmānyaṃ
                        vaiśeṣikaṃ ca | śyāvaṃ piḍakācitaṃ śophavedanāvantaṃ muhurmuhuḥ
                        śoṇitāsrāviṇaṃ budbudavad unnataṃ mṛdumāṃsaṃ ca vraṇaṃ jānīyāt saśalyo 'yam
                        iti | sāmānyam etal lakṣaṇam uktam | vaiśeṣikaṃ tu tvaggate vivarṇaḥ śopho
                        bhavaty āyataḥ kaṭhinaś ca māṃsagate śophābhivṛddhiḥ śalyamārgānupasaṃrohaḥ
                        pīḍanāsahiṣṇutā coṣapākau ca peśyantarasthe 'py etad eva coṣaśophavarjaṃ
                        sirāgate sirādhmānam sirāśūlaṃ sirāśophaś ca snāyugate snāyujālotkṣepaṇaṃ
                        saṃrambhaś cogrā ruk ca srotogate srotasāṃ svakarmaguṇahāniḥ; dhamanīsthe
                        saphenaṃ raktam īrayann anilaḥ saśabdo nirgacchaty aṅgamardaḥ pipāsā
                        hṛllāsaś ca asthigate vividhavedanāprādurbhāvaḥ śophaś ca asthivivaragate
                        'sthipūrṇatā'sthitodaḥ saṃharṣo balavāṃś ca sandhigate 'sthivacceṣṭoparamaś
                        ca koṣṭhagata āṭopānāhau mūtrapurīṣāhāradarśanaṃ ca vraṇamukhāt marmagate
                        marmaviddhāvac ceṣṭate | sūkṣmagatiṣu śalyeṣv etāny eva lakṣaṇāny aspaṣṭāni
                        bhavanti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.26.11">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.26.11</label>
                         mahānty alpāni vā śuddhadehānām anulomasanniviṣṭāni rohanti viśeṣataḥ
                        kaṇṭhasrotaḥsirātvakpeśyasthivivareṣu doṣaprakopavyāyāmābhighātājīrṇebhyaḥ
                        pracalitāni punarbādhante || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.26.12">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.26.12</label>
                         tatra tvakpranaṣṭe snigdhasvinnāyāṃ mṛnmāṣayavagodhūmagomayamṛditāyāṃ tvaci
                        yatra saṃrambho vedanā vā bhavati tatra śalyaṃ vijānīyāt
                        styānaghṛtamṛccandanakalkair vā pradigdhāyāṃ śalyoṣmaṇā+āśu visarati ghṛtam
                        upaśuṣyati vā lepo yatra tatra śalyaṃ vijānīyāt māṃsapranaṣṭe
                        snehasvedādibhiḥ kriyāviśeṣair aviruddair āturam upapādayet karśitasya tu
                        śithilībhūtam anavabaddhaṃ kṣubhyamāṇaṃ yatra saṃrambhaṃ vedanāṃ vā janayati
                        tatra śalyaṃ vijānīyāt koṣṭhāsthisandhipeśīvivareṣv avasthitam evam eva
                        parīkṣeta sirādhamanīsrotaḥsnāyupranaṣṭe khaṇḍacakrasaṃyukte yāne vyādhitam
                        āropyāśu viṣame 'dhvani yāyād yatra saṃrambho vedanā vā bhavati tatra śalyaṃ
                        jānīyāt asthipranaṣṭe snehasvedopapannānyasthīni bandhanapīḍanābhyāṃ bhṛśam
                        upācared yatra saṃrambho vedanā vā bhavati tatra śalyaṃ jānīyāt
                        sandhipranaṣṭe snehasvedopapannān sandhīn prasaraṇākuñcanabandhanapīḍanair
                        bhṛśam upācaret yatra saṃrambho vedanā vā bhavati tatra śalyaṃ vijānīyāt
                        marmapranaṣṭe tv ananyabhāvān marmaṇām uktaṃ parīkṣaṇaṃ bhavati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.26.13">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.26.13</label>
                         sāmānyalakṣaṇam api ca
                        hastiskandhāśvapṛṣṭhaparvatadrumārohaṇadhanurvyāyāmadrutayānaniyuddhādhvagamanalaṅghanaprataraṇaplavanavyāyāmair
                        jṛmbhodgārakāsakṣavathuṣṭhīvanahasanaprāṇāyāmair
                        vātamūtrapurīṣaśukrotsargair vā yatra saṃrambho vedanā vā bhavati tatra
                        śalyaṃ jānīyāt || </l>



                    <l xml:id="SS.1.26.14"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.26.15">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.26.15</label>
                         bhavanti cātra |
                        <caesura/>
                         āturaś cāpi yaṃ deśam abhīkṣṇaṃ parirakṣati |
                        <caesura/>
                         saṃvāhyamāno bahuśas tatra śalyaṃ vinirdiśet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.26.16">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.26.16</label>
                         alpābādham aśūnaṃ ca nīrujaṃ nirupadravam |
                        <caesura/>
                         prasannaṃ mṛduparyantaṃ nirāghaṭṭamanunnatam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.26.17">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.26.17</label>
                         eṣaṇyā sarvato dṛṣṭvā yathāmārgaṃ cikitsakaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         prasārākuñcanān nūnaṃ niḥśalyam iti nirdiśet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.26.18">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.26.18</label>
                         asthyātmakaṃ bhajyate tu śalyamantaś ca śīryate |
                        <caesura/>
                         prāyo nirbhujyate śārṅgam āyasaṃ ceti niścayaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.26.19">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.26.19</label>
                         vārkṣavaiṇavatārṇāni nirhrayante tu no yadi |
                        <caesura/>
                         pacanti raktaṃ māṃsaṃ ca kṣipram etāni dehinām || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.26.20">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.26.20</label>
                         kānakaṃ rājataṃ tāmraṃ raitikaṃ trapusīsakam |
                        <caesura/>
                         cirasthānād vilīyante pittatejaḥpratāpanāt || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.26.21">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.26.21</label>
                         svabhāvaśītā mṛdavo ye cānye 'pīdṛśā matāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         dravībhūtāḥ śarīre 'sminn ekatvaṃ yānti dhātubhiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.26.22">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.26.22</label>
                         viṣāṇadantakeśāsthiveṇudārūpalāni tu |
                        <caesura/>
                         śalyāni na viśīryante śarīre mṛnmayāni ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.26.23">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.26.23</label>
                         dvividhaṃ pañcagatimattvagādivraṇavastuṣu |
                        <caesura/>
                         viśliṣṭaṃ vetti yaḥ śalyaṃ sa rājñaḥ kartum arhati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.26.trailer">iti suśrtasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne
                        pranaṣṭaśalyavijñānīyo nāma ṣaḍviṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ || </l>
                </div>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.27.1">

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.27.3">

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.27.4">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.27.4</label>
                         tatra samāsenānavabaddhaśalyoddharaṇārthaṃ pañcadaśa hetūn vakṣyāmaḥ | tad
                        yathā svabhāvaḥ pācanaṃ bhedanaṃ dāraṇaṃ pīḍanaṃ pramārjanaṃ nirdhmāpanaṃ
                        vamanaṃ virecanaṃ prakṣālanaṃ pratimarśaḥ pravāhaṇaṃ ācūṣaṇaṃ ayaskānto
                        harṣaś ceti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.27.5">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.27.5</label>
                         tatrāśrukṣavathūdgārakāsamūtrapurīṣānilaiḥ svabhāvabalapravṛttair
                        nayanādibhyaḥ patati māṃsāvagāḍhaṃ śalyamavidahyamānaṃ pācayitvā
                        prakothā(ā.pā)ttasya pūyaśoṇitavegād gauravād vā patati | pakvamabhidyamānaṃ
                        bhedayed dārayed vā | bhinnamanirasyamānaṃ pīḍanīyaiḥ pīḍayet pāṇibhir vā |
                        aṇūny akṣaśalyāni pariṣecanādhmāpanair bālavastrapāṇibhiḥ pramārjayet |
                        āhāraśeṣaśleṣmahīnāṇuśalyāni śvasanotkāsanapradhamanair nirdhamet |
                        annaśalyāni vamanāṅgulipratimarśaprabhṛtibhiḥ | virecanaiḥ pakvāśayagatāni |
                        vraṇadoṣāśayagatāni prakṣālanaiḥ | vātamūtrapurīṣagarbhasaṅgeṣu
                        pravāhaṇamuktaṃ | mārutodakasaviṣarudhiraduṣṭastanyeṣv ācūṣaṇam āsyena
                        viṣāṇair vā | anulomam anavabaddham akarṇam analpavraṇamukham ayaskāntena |
                        hṛdy avasthitam anekakāraṇotpannaṃ śokaśalyaṃ harṣeṇeti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.27.6">

                        'nulomaś ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.27.7-8">

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.27.10">

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.27.11">

                        <caesura/>
                         śītalena jalenainaṃ mūrcchantam avasecayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         saṃrakṣedasya marmāṇi muhur āśvāsayec ca tam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.27.12">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.27.12</label>
                         tataḥ śalyam uddhṛtya nirlohitaṃ vraṇaṃ kṛtvā svedārham
                        agnighṛtaprabhṛtibhiḥ saṃsvedya vidahya pradihya sarpirmadhubhyāṃ
                        baddhvā+ācārikam upadiśet | (? sirāsnāyuvilagnaṃ śalākādibhir vimocyāpanayet
                        śvayathugrastavāraṅgaṃ samavapīḍya śvayathuṃ durbalavāraṅgaṃ kuśādibhir
                        baddhvā |) </l>

                        yathāmārgaṃ durupaharamanyato 'pabādhyamānaṃ pāṭayitvoddharet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.27.14">

                        aśakyamevaṃ vā balavadbhiḥ suparigṛhītasya yantreṇa grāhayitvā śalyavāraṅgaṃ
                        pravibhujya dhanurguṇair baddhaikataś cāsya pañcāṅgyām upasaṃyatasyāśvasya
                        vaktrakavike badhnīyāt athainaṃ kaśayā tāḍayed yathonnamayan śiro vegena
                        śalyam uddharati dṛḍhāṃ vā vṛkṣaśākhām avanamya tasyāṃ pūrvavad
                        baddhvoddharet || </l>

                        śītābhir adbhiḥ pariṣicya sthirībhūtām uddharet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.27.18-21">

                        vāmayet vamataś ca śalyaikadeśasaktaṃ jñātvā sūtraṃ sahasā tvākṣipet mṛdunā
                        vā dantadhāvanakūrcakenāpaharet praṇudedvā'ntaḥ | kṣatakaṇṭhāya ca
                        madhusarpiṣī leḍhuṃ prayacchettriphalācūrṇaṃ vā madhuśarkarāvimiśram ||
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.27.20</label>
                         udakapūrṇodaramavākśirasamavapīḍayed dhunīyādvāmayed vā bhasmarāśau vā
                        nikhanedāmukhāt ||
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.27.21</label>
                         grāsaśalye tu kaṇṭhāsakte niḥśaṅkamanavabuddhaṃ skandhe muṣṭinā'bhihanyāt
                        snehaṃ madyaṃ pānīyaṃ vā pāyayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.27.22">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.27.22</label>

                        niruṇaddhi lālāsrāvaṃ phenāgamanaṃ saṃjñānāśaṃ cāpādayati tamabhyajya
                        saṃsvedya śirovirecanaṃ tasmai tīkṣṇaṃ dadyādrasaṃ ca vātaghnaṃ vidadhyād
                        iti || </l>

                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>

                <div n="28" type="adhyāya">
                    <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 28, collation]</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.28.1">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.28.1</label>
                         athāto viparītavraṇavijñānīyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.28.3">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.28.3</label>
                         phalāgnijalavṛṣṭīnāṃ puṣpadhūmāmbudā yathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         khyāpayanti bhaviṣyatvaṃ riṣṭāni maraṇan tathā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.28.4">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.28.4</label>
                         tāni saukṣmyāt pramādād vā tathaivāśu vyatikramāt |
                        <caesura/>
                         gṛhyante nodgatāny ajñair mumūrṣor na tv asaṃbhavāt || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.28.5">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.28.5</label>
                         dhruvaṃ tu maraṇaṃ riṣṭe brāhmaṇais tat kilāmalaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         rasāyanatapojapyatatparair vā nivāryate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.28.6">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.28.6</label>
                         nakṣatrapīḍā bahudhā yathā kālād vipacyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         tathaivāriṣṭapākaṃ ca bruvate bahavo janāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.28.7">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.28.7</label>
                         asiddhim āpnuyāl loke pratikurvan gatāyuṣaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         ato 'riṣṭani yatnena lakṣayet kuśalo bhiṣak || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.28.8">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.28.8</label>
                         gandhavarṇarasādīnāṃ viśeṣāṇāṃ svabhāvataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         vaikṛtaṃ yat tad ācaṣṭe vraṇinaḥ pakvalakṣaṇam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.28.9">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.28.9</label>
                         kaṭus tīkṣṇaś ca visraś ca gandhas tu pavanādibhiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         lohagandhis tu raktena vyāmiśraḥ sānnipātikaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.28.10">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.28.10</label>
                         lājātasītailasamāḥ kiṃcidvisrāś ca gandhataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         jñeyāḥ prakṛtigandhāḥ syur ato 'nyad gandhavaikṛtam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.28.11">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.28.11</label>
                         madhyāgurvājyasumanaḥpadmacandanacampakaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sagandhā divyagandhāś ca mumūrṣūṇāṃ vraṇāḥ smṛtāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.28.12">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.28.12</label>
                         śvavājimūṣikadhvāṅkṣapūtivallūramatkuṇaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sagandhāḥ paṅkagandhāś ca bhūmigandhāś ca garhitāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.28.13">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.28.13</label>
                         kuṅkumadhyāmakaṃguṣṭhaḥ savarṇṇāḥ pittajāś ca ye |
                        <caesura/>
                         na dahyante śuṣyanti varjjayet tān vicakṣaṇaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.28.14">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.28.14</label>
                         kaṇḍūmantaḥ sthirāḥ śvetāḥ snigdhāḥ kaphanimittataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         dūyante vā'pi dahyante bhiṣak tān parivarjayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.28.15">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.28.15</label>
                         kṛṣṇās tu ye tanusrāvā vātajā marmatāpinaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         svalpām api na kurvanti rujaṃ tān parivarjayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.28.16">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.28.16</label>
                         kṣveḍanti ghurghurāyante jvalantīva ca ye vraṇāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tvaṅmāṃsasthāś ca pavanaṃ saśabdaṃ visṛjanti ye || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.28.17">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.28.17</label>
                         ye ca marmasvasaṃbhūtā bhavanty atyarthavedanāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         dahyante cāntaratyarthaṃ bahiḥ śītāś ca ye vraṇāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.28.18">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.28.18</label>
                         dahyante bahir atyarthaṃ bhavanty antaś ca śītalāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śaktidhvajarathā kuntavājivāraṇagovṛṣāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.28.19">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.28.19</label>
                         yeṣu cāpy avabhāseran prāsādākṛtayas tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         cūrṇāvakīrṇā iva ye bhānti vā na ca cūrṇitāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.28.20">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.28.20</label>
                         prāṇamāṃsakṣayaśvāsakāsārocakapīḍitāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         pravṛddhapūyarudhirā vraṇā yeṣāṃ ca marmasu || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.28.21">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.28.21</label>
                         kriyābhiḥ samyag ārabdhā na sidhyanti ca ye vraṇāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         varjayet tān bhiṣak prājñaḥ saṃrakṣannātmano yaśaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.28.trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne
                        viparītāviparītavraṇavijñānīyo nāmāṣṭaviṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.29.1">

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.29.3">

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.29.6">

                         napuṃsakaṃ strī bahavo naikakāryā asūyakāḥ |

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.29.78">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.29.78</label>
                         mahāprāsādasaphalavṛkṣavāraṇaparvatān |
                        <caesura/>
                         āroheddravyalābhāya vyādherapagamāya ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.29.79">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.29.79</label>
                         nadīnadasamudrāṃś ca kṣubhitān kaluṣodakān |
                        <caesura/>
                         taret kalyāṇalābhāya vyādher apagamāya ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.29.79cdI"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.29.79cdII"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.29.80">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.29.80</label>
                         urago vā jalauko vā bhramaro vā'pi yaṃ daśet |
                        <caesura/>
                         ārogyaṃ nirdiśettasya dhanalābhaṃ ca buddhimān || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.29.81">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.29.81</label>
                         evaṃrūpān śubhān svapnān yaḥ paśyed vyādhito naraḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sa dīrghāyur iti jñeyas tasmai karma samācaret || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.29.trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne
                        viparītāviparītasvapnanidarśanīyo nāmaikonatriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ || </l>
                </div>


                <div n="30" type="adhyāya">
                    <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 30, collation]</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.30.1">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.30.1</label>
                         athātaḥ pañcendriyārthavipratipattim adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>



                    <l xml:id="SS.1.30.3">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.30.3</label>
                         śarīraśīlayor yasya prakṛter vikṛtir bhavet |
                        <caesura/>
                         tat tva riṣṭaṃ samāsena vyāsatas tu nibodha me || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.30.4">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.30.4</label>
                         śṛṇoti vividhān śabdān yo divyānām abhāvataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         samudrapurameghānām asaṃpattau ca niḥsvanān || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.30.5">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.30.5</label>
                         tān svanānnāvagṛhṇāti manyate cānyaśabdavat |
                        <caesura/>
                         grāmyāraṇyasvanāṃś cāpi viparītān śṛṇoti ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.30.6">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.30.6</label>
                         dviṣacchabdeṣu ramate suhṛcchabdeṣu kupyati |
                        <caesura/>
                         na śṛṇoti ca yo 'kasmāttaṃ bruvanti gatāyuṣam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.30.7">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.30.7</label>
                         yat tūṣṇam iti gṛhṇāti śītam uṣṇaṃ ca śītavat |
                        <caesura/>
                         saṃjātaśītapiḍako yaś ca dāhena pīḍyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.30.8">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.30.8</label>
                         uṣṇagātro 'tigātrañ ca yaḥ śītena pravepate |
                        <caesura/>
                         prahārān nābhijānāti yo 'ṅgacchedam athāpi vā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.30.9">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.30.9</label>
                         pāṃśunaivāvakīrṇāni yaś ca gātrāṇi manyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         varṇānyatā vā rājyo vā yasya gātre bhavanti hi || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.30.10">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.30.10</label>
                         snātānuliptaṃ yaṃ cāpi bhajante nīlamakṣikāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sugandhirvā'ti yo 'kasmāt taṃ bruvanti gatāyuṣam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.30.11">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.30.11</label>
                         viparītena gṛhṇāti rasān yaś copayojitān |
                        <caesura/>
                         upayuktāḥ kramādyasya rasā doṣābhivṛddhaye || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.30.12">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.30.12</label>
                         yasya doṣāgnisāmyaṃ ca kuryur mithyopayojitāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yo vā rasān na saṃvetti gatāsuṃ taṃ pracakṣate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.30.13">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.30.13</label>
                         sugandhaṃ vetti durgandhaṃ durgandhasya sugandhitām |
                        <caesura/>
                         gṛhṇīte vā 'nyathā gandhaṃ śānte dīpe ca nīrujaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.30.14"/>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.30.15"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.30.16">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.30.16</label>
                         rātrau sūryaṃ jvalantaṃ vā divā vā candravarcasam |
                        <caesura/>
                         ameghopaplave yaś ca śakracāpataḍidguṇān || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.30.17">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.30.17</label>
                         taḍittvato 'sitān yo vā nirmale gagane ghanān |
                        <caesura/>
                         vimānayānaprāsādair yaś ca saṃkulamambaram || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.30.18">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.30.18</label>
                         yaś cānilaṃ mūrtimantam antarikṣaṃ ca paśyati |
                        <caesura/>
                         dhūmanīhāravāsobhir āvṛtām iva medinīm || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.30.19">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.30.19</label>
                         pradīptam iva lokaṃ ca yo vā plutam ivāmbhasā |
                        <caesura/>
                         bhūmim aṣṭāpadākārāṃ lekhābhir yaś ca paśyati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.30.23">
                        <label>1.30.23</label>
                         yo vā mayūrakaṇṭhābhaṃ vidhūmam vahnim īkṣate |
                        <caesura/>
                         dhruvam ākāśagaṅgāṃ vā taṃ bruvanti gatāyuṣaṃ </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.30.21">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.30.21</label>
                         jyotsnādarśoṣṇatoyeṣu chāyāṃ yaś ca na paśyati |
                        <caesura/>
                         paśyaty ekāṅgahīnāṃ vā vikṛtāṃ vā'nyasattvajām || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.30.22">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.30.22</label>
                         śvakākakaṅkagṛdhrāṇāṃ pretānāṃ yakṣarakṣasām |
                        <caesura/>
                         piśācoraganāgānāṃ bhūtānāṃ vikṛtām api || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.30.22.1">
                        <label>1.30.22.1</label>
                         svasthaḥ sa labhate vyādhiṃ vyādhi<cb/>to mṛtyum arcchati || ||
                        <caesura/>
                         vraṇapraśnam vraṇāsrāvaṃ kṛtyākṛtyavidhin tathā | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.30.22.2">
                        <label>1.30.22.2</label>
                         vyādhyuddeśīyam adhyāyaṃ śastrakarmmāṣṭakan tathā ||
                        <caesura/>
                         praṇaṣṭaśalyavijñānaṃ śalyāpanayanam eva ca | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.30.22.3">
                        <label>1.30.22.3</label>
                         viparītavraṇajñānaṃ dūtasvapnaviparyayaṃ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         pañcendriyārthavibhrāntim proktaṃ vai tṛtīyo daśa || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.30.trailer">|| 30 || </l>
                </div>

                <div n="31" type="adhyāya">
                    <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 31, collation]</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.1">
                        <label>1.31.1</label>
                         athātaś cchāyāvipratipattim vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.3">
                        <label>1.31.3</label>
                         śyāvā lohitikā nīlāḥ pītikā vāpi dehināṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         abhidravanti yañ chāyā sa parāsur asaṃśayaṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.4">
                        <label>1.31.4</label>
                         hrīr apakrāmati yataḥ kāntismṛtidhṛtiśriyaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         akasmād yaṃ bhajante ca sa parāsur asaṃśayam | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.5">
                        <label>1.31.5</label>
                         yasyādharauṣṭhaḥ patitaḥ kṣiptaś cordhan tathottaraḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         ubhau vā jāmbavābhāsau sa parāsur asaṃśayam | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.6">
                        <label>1.31.6</label>
                         āraktā daśanā yasya śyāvā vā syuḥ patanti vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         khāñjanapratibho vāpi taṃ gatāyuṣam ādiśet | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.7">
                        <label>1.31.7</label>
                         kṛṣṇā snigdhāvaliptā vā jihvā śūnā ca yasya vai |
                        <caesura/>
                         karkaśā ca bhaved yasya so cirād vijahāty asūn | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.8">
                        <label>1.31.8</label>
                         kuṭilā sphuṭitā vāpi śūnā vā yasya nāsikā |
                        <caesura/>
                         bhagnā vā sphurate vāpi sa parāsur asaṃśayaṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.9">
                        <label>1.31.9</label>
                         saṃkṣipte viṣame stabdhe rakte supte ca locane |
                        <caesura/>
                         yasya syātāṃ śrute vāpi sa parāsur asaṃśayaṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.10"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.11">
                        <label>1.31.11</label>
                         na dhārayati yaḥ śīrṣan nāharanty annam āsyagaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         ekāgradṛṣṭir mūḍhātmā sa parāsur asaṃśayaṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.12">
                        <label>1.31.12</label>
                         balavān durbalo vāpi sammohaṃ yo dhigacchati |
                        <caesura/>
                         utthāpyamāno bahuśaḥ sa parāsur asaṃśayaṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.13">
                        <label>1.31.13</label>
                         uttānaḥ sarvadā śete | pādau vikurute ca yaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         viprasāraṇaśīlo vā sa parāsur asaṃśayaṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.14">
                        <label>1.31.14</label>
                         śītapādakarocchvāsaḥ chinnaśvāsaś ca yo bhavet |
                        <caesura/>
                         kākocchvāsaś ca yo martyaḥ sa parāsur asaṃśayaṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.15">
                        <label>1.31.15</label>
                         nidrā na cchidyate yasya yo vā jāgartti sarvadā |
                        <caesura/>
                         muhyed vā vaktukāmaś ca pratyākhyeyaḥ sa jānatā | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.16">
                        <label>1.31.16</label>
                         parilihed uttaroṣṭham uṅgarāṃś ca karoti vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         pretair vā bhāṣate sārdhaṃ sa parāsur asaṃśayaṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.17">
                        <label>1.31.17</label>
                         khebhyaḥ saromakūpebhyo yasya raktaṃ pravarttate |
                        <caesura/>
                         puruṣasyāviṣārttasya sa parāsur asaṃśayaṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.18">
                        <label>1.31.18</label>
                         vātāṣṭhīlā tu hṛdaye yasyordhvam anuyāyinī |
                        <caesura/>
                         rujānnavidveṣakarī sa parāsur asaṃśayaṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.19">
                        <label>1.31.19</label>
                         ananyopadravakṛtaḥ pādaḥ śophaḥ samutthitaḥ
                        <caesura/>
                         puruṣaṃ hanti nārīñ ca mukhajo guhyajo dvayaṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.20">
                        <label>1.31.20</label>
                         atīsāro jvaro dhmānaṃ charddiḥ śūnāṅgameḍhratā |
                        <caesura/>
                         kāsina svāsino vāpi yasya taṃ kṣīṇam ādiśet | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.21">
                        <label>1.31.21</label>
                         svedo dāhaś ca balavāṃ hikkā śvāsaś ca mānavaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         balavantam api prāṇair viyuñjanti na saṃśayaṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.22">
                        <label>1.31.22</label>
                         śyāvā jihvā bhaved yasya savyaṃ cākṣi nimajjati
                        <caesura/>
                         mukhaṃ ca jāyate pūtir yasya taṃ parivarjayet | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.23">
                        <label>1.31.23</label>
                         netre cāmreṇa pūryete svidyete caraṇau tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         cakṣuś cākulatāṃ yāti yamarāṣṭraṃ gamiṣyataḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.24">
                        <label>1.31.24</label>
                         atimātraṃ laghūni syur gātrāṇy atigurūṇi vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         yasyākasmāt sa vijñeyo gantā caiva yamālayaṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.25">
                        <label>1.31.25</label>
                         paṅkamatsyavasātailaghṛtagandhāś ca ye narāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         piṣṭagandhāṃś ca ye vānti gatās te yamasādanaṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.26">
                        <label>1.31.26</label>
                         yūkā lalāṭam āyānti balin nāśnanti vāyasāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yeṣāñ cāpi ratin nāsti gatās te yamasādanaṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.27">
                        <label>1.31.27</label>
                         jvarātīsāraśophā syur yasyānyonyāvasādinaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         prakṣīṇañ ca balaṃ yasya na sa śakyaś cikitsituṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.28">
                        <label>1.31.28</label>
                         kṣīṇasya yasya kṣuttṛṣṇe hṛdyair mṛṣṭair hitais tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         annapānair nna sāsyete tasya mṛtyur upasthitaḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.29">
                        <label>1.31.29</label>
                         pravāhikā śiraḥśūlaṃ koṣṭhaśūlaś ca dāruṇa |
                        <caesura/>
                         pipāsā balahāniś ca tasya mṛtyur upasthitaḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.30">
                        <label>1.31.30</label>
                         viṣameṇopacāreṇa karmabhiś ca purākṛtaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         anityatvāc ca jantūnāṃ jīvitaṃ nidhanam vrajet | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.31">
                        <label>1.31.31</label>
                         pretā dūtāḥ piśācāś ca rakṣāṃsi vividhāni ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         maraṇīyan naran nityam upasarpanti sarvadā </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.32">
                        <label>1.31.32</label>
                         tāni bheṣajavīryāṇi pratinighnanti sarvadā |
                        <caesura/>
                         tasmān mohāḥ kriyās sarvā bhavantīha gatāyuṣam iti || 31 || </l>



                </div>


            </div>
